# Rubrics 1960 2026 Compositor Divergences

This file tracks the current **legacy Perl rendered Hour vs compositor** comparison state for `Rubrics 1960 - 1960`.

## Current status

- Comparison surface:
  - live Perl helper: `packages/compositor/test/fixtures/officium-content-snapshot.pl`
  - live harness: `pnpm -C packages/compositor compare:phase-3-perl -- --version "Rubrics 1960 - 1960" --year 2026`
  - dates: `365` dates in `2026`
  - hours: `Matins, Lauds, Prime, Terce, Sext, None, Vespers, Compline`
  - language: `Latin`
- Compared hours: `2920`
- Exact-match hours: `1008`
- Divergent hours: `1912`
- Divergent dates: `354`
- Best matching prefix before divergence: `385` lines
- Average matching prefix before divergence: `48.0` lines
- Divergence breakdown by hour:
  - `Matins`: `334/365`
  - `Lauds`: `284/365`
  - `Prime`: `297/365`
  - `Terce`: `203/365`
  - `Sext`: `188/365`
  - `None`: `195/365`
  - `Vespers`: `305/365`
  - `Compline`: `106/365`
- Adjudication breakdown (see `adjudications.json` and ADR-011):
  - `unadjudicated`: `797`
  - `perl-bug`: `1115`

## Notes

- This ledger is auto-generated by `compare-phase-3-perl.mjs` on every run. **Do not hand-edit** the table — edits are lost.
- Adjudications live in `packages/compositor/test/divergence/adjudications.json` and are merged into the `Class` / `Citation` columns by the harness. See [ADR-011](../../../../docs/adr/011-phase-3-divergence-adjudication.md) for the key schema and classification protocol.
- The four row classes are `engine-bug`, `perl-bug`, `ordo-ambiguous`, and `rendering-difference`. Rows without an adjudication entry surface as `unadjudicated`.
- Per CLAUDE.md §19.4 and ADR-011: no divergence is ever resolved by "matching the Perl" alone. Every adjudication carries a citation.
